<script>

    (function(){



        KISSY.use('node,io',function(S,D,IO){



            var util = TB.Global.util;

            var footerSite = D.all('.footer-site a');

            var NationCookie = {
                'CN' : ['CN_zh-cn_CHN'],
                'TW' : ['TW_zh-tw_TWD'],
                'HK' : ['HK_zh-tw_HKD'],
                'MO' : ['MO_zh-tw_MOP'],
                'SG' : ['SG_zh-cn_SGD'],
                'MY' : ['MY_zh-cn_MYR'],
                'US' : ['US_zh-cn_USD'],
                'CA' : ['CA_zh-cn_CAD'],
                'AU' : ['AU_zh-cn_AUD'],
                'NZ' : ['NZ_zh-cn_NZD'],
                'JP' : ['JP_zh-cn_JPY'],
                'KR' : ['KR_zh-cn_KER'],
                'XX' : ['XX_zh-cn_USD']
            };



            S.each(footerSite,function(site){

                var siteElem = D.one(site);

                siteElem.on('click',function(e){

                    e.preventDefault();



                    var Nation = siteElem.attr('data-nation');

                    var CookieUrl = util.isDaily() ? '//gskip.daily.taobao.net/json/processUserCookie.htm?from=1&site=' : '//gskip.taobao.com/json/processUserCookie.htm?from=1&site=';

                    var NationUrl = CookieUrl + NationCookie[Nation][0] + '&t=' + S.now();

                    var syncCookie = (util.isDaily() ? '//jump.daily.taobao.net/jump?target=' : '//login.taobao.com/jump?target=') + 'ht'+'tps'+'://www.tmall.com';

                    new IO({
                        dataType: 'jsonp',
                        url: NationUrl,
                        success: function(data){

                            if(!data.ret) return;

                            
                          S.getScript(syncCookie,function(){
                            if(Nation === 'CN' || Nation === 'TW' ){

                                var href = Nation === 'CN' ? '//www.taobao.com' : '//tw.taobao.com';
                                location.href = href;
                                return;
                            }
                            location.reload();
                          });
                            

                            
                        }
                    });


                });


            });



        });




    })()


</script>

        <script>
(function() {
    var doc = document, con = doc.getElementById('content') || doc,
        as = con.getElementsByTagName('a'), len = as.length, i = 0, a,
        SPECIALS = /([.\/?])/g,
        unsafeUrls = [
            'member1.taobao.com/member/loginByIm.do',
            'jp.rd.yahoo.com/SIG=10uaccr0v/D=maps/Y=YAHOO/EXP=1288992407/'
        ],
        REG = new RegExp('(' + unsafeUrls.join(')|(').replace(SPECIALS, '\\$1') + ')');
    
    for(; i < len; ++i) {
        a = as[i];
        if (REG.test(a.href)) {
            a.href = '#';
        }
    }
})();
</script>

    
    
            <script>
    var host = window.location.host;
    var parts = host.split(".");
    var hostPartsLen = parts.length;
    var mainHost = ""
    for(var i=0; i<hostPartsLen;i++){
        if (i == 0){
            mainHost = parts[i]
        }
        else if(i== 1){
            continue;
        }else {
            mainHost = mainHost + "." + parts[i];
        }
    }

    var processATag = function(node, index){
        var href = node.href;
        if (href.match(mainHost)) {
            node.href = href.replace(mainHost, host);
        }
    }

    var processFormTag = function(node, index){
        var action = node.action;
        if (action.match(mainHost)) {
            node.action = action.replace(mainHost, host);
        }
    }
    KISSY.use('node', function (S, Node) {
        var hrefNodes = Node.all("[href]");
        S.each(hrefNodes, processATag);

        var formNodes = Node.all("form");
        S.each(formNodes, processFormTag);

        Node.all('.J_TModule').on('click', function (e) {
            var urlReplaced = this.getAttribute("data-worldsite-url-replaced");

            if(!urlReplaced){
                var id = this.id;
                var prefix = "#" + id;

                var aTagNodes = S.all(prefix + " a");
                S.each(aTagNodes, processATag);

                var formTagNodes = S.all(prefix + " form");
                S.each(formTagNodes, processFormTag);

                this.setAttribute("data-worldsite-url-replaced",true);
            }


        });
    });
</script>

        function addEvent(elm, evType, fn, useCapture) {
            if (elm.addEventListener) {
                elm.addEventListener(evType, fn, useCapture); //DOM2.0
                return true;
            } else if (elm.attachEvent) {
                var r = elm.attachEvent("on" + evType, fn);
                return r;
            }
        }

        var timer;
        addEvent(window, "scroll", function() {
            clearTimeout(timer);
            timer = setTimeout(function() {
                embedReplace && embedReplace.replaceAll(); //eslint-disable-line
            }, 300);
        });
    }());
